              /checkout\//,
              /order-details/,
              /privacy-policy/,
              /profile-page\//
          ];
      
          // Check if any regex in popupExcludeArr matches current URL
          const shouldExclude = popupExcludeArr.some(regex => regex.test(currentUrl));

              console.log("Popup excluded for this URL:", currentUrl);

                      function pushEvent(eventName) {
                          window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
                          dataLayer.push({ event: eventName });
                          console.log("Pushed:", eventName);
                      }
      
                      function handlePermissionChange(newState) {
                          console.log("Permission changed to:", newState);
      
                          if (newState === "granted") {
                              pushEvent("web_push_subscribed");     // Allow clicked
                          }
                          else if (newState === "denied") {
                              pushEvent("web_push_denied");         // Block clicked
                          }
                          else if (newState === "default") {
                              pushEvent("web_push_banner_Closed");  // Closed without choosing
                          }
                      }
      
                      // Try Permissions API first
                      function setupPermissionWatcher() {
                          if (navigator.permissions && navigator.permissions.query) {
                              navigator.permissions.query({ name: "notifications" })
                                  .then(function (status) {
                                      handlePermissionChange(status.state);
      
                                      status.onchange = function () {
                                          handlePermissionChange(this.state);
                                      };
                                  })
                                  .catch(startPollingFallback);
                          } else {
                              startPollingFallback();
                          }
                      }
      
                      // Fallback polling for browsers that block Permissions API for notifications
                      var pollId = null;
                      function startPollingFallback() {
                          var last = Notification.permission;
      
                          pollId = setInterval(function () {
                              var current = Notification.permission;
                              if (current !== last) {
                                  last = current;
                                  handlePermissionChange(current);
                              }
                          }, 1200);
                      }
      
                      setupPermissionWatcher();
                  })();
              } catch (error) {
                  console.log(error);
              }
          }, 10000);
      })

                        <h2>Frequently Asked Questions</h2>
                    </div>

                <div class="accordionsinglequestion" bis_skin_checked="1">
                    <section class="accordion-item open">
                        <h3 class="accordion-header active">
                            <span class="accordion-title">1. Apa itu NONO4D?</span>
                            <span class="accordion-icon"></span>
                        </h3>
                        <div class="accordion-panel expanded" style="height: 88px;" bis_skin_checked="1">
                            <div class="answer" bis_skin_checked="1">
                                <p></p>
                                <p>NONO4D adalah bandar toto slot resmi Indonesia yang menyediakan link agen slot gacor malam ini dengan jaminan akses super cepat, pasaran terlengkap, dan peluang menang jackpot paling besar.</p>
                                <p></p>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </section>
                    <section class="accordion-item open">
                        <h3 class="accordion-header active">
                            <span class="accordion-title">2. Kenapa harus memilih NONO4D sebagai tempat bermain?</span>
                            <span class="accordion-icon"></span>
                        </h3>
                        <div class="accordion-panel expanded" style="height: 88px;" bis_skin_checked="1">
                            <div class="answer" bis_skin_checked="1">
                                <p></p>
                                <p>Karena NONO4D merupakan bandar toto slot resmi Indonesia terpercaya yang selalu memperbarui link agen slot gacor malam ini demi memastikan keamanan taruhan, bonus melimpah, dan server stabil anti lag.</p>
                                <p></p>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </section>
                    <section class="accordion-item open">
                        <h3 class="accordion-header active">
                            <span class="accordion-title">3. Bagaimana cara mendapatkan info slot gacor di NONO4D?</span>
                            <span class="accordion-icon"></span>
                        </h3>
                        <div class="accordion-panel expanded" style="height: 88px;" bis_skin_checked="1">
                            <div class="answer" bis_skin_checked="1">
                                <p></p>
                                <p>Anda cukup mengakses link agen slot gacor malam ini yang disediakan oleh NONO4D. Sebagai bandar toto slot resmi Indonesia, kami menyajikan bocoran game RTP tinggi yang gampang maxwin setiap harinya.</p>
                                <p></p>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </section>
                    <section class="accordion-item open">
                        <h3 class="accordion-header active">
                            <span class="accordion-title">4. Apakah link agen slot gacor malam ini di NONO4D aman diakses?</span>
                            <span class="accordion-icon"></span>
                        </h3>
                        <div class="accordion-panel expanded" style="height: 88px;" bis_skin_checked="1">

                                <p></p>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </section>

                        <h3 class="accordion-header active">

                            <span class="accordion-icon"></span>
                        </h3>
                        <div class="accordion-panel expanded" style="height: 88px;" bis_skin_checked="1">

    <span class="snowflake " style="left: 96.7816vw; --delay: -11.60s; --dur: 10.71s; --sway: 8.82s; --drift: 36.5px; --rot: 42deg; --scale: 1.13; --blur: 0.9px; --glow: 20px; top: -1.97829vh;"></span>

<!-- opsional: auto-generate 120 keping salju -->
<script>
    (function() {
        const wrap = document.getElementById('snow');
        if (!wrap)
            return;

        const COUNT = 120;
        // 80â€“160 paling aman untuk mobile

        for (let i = 0; i < COUNT; i++) {
            const f = document.createElement('span');

            const r = Math.random();
            let sizeClass = '';
            if (r < 0.18)
                sizeClass = '-lg';
            else if (r < 0.65)
                sizeClass = '-sm';

            f.className = 'snowflake ' + sizeClass;

            const left = Math.random() * 100;
            const delay = (Math.random() * -14).toFixed(2) + 's';
            const dur = (7 + Math.random() * 11).toFixed(2) + 's';
            const sway = (3 + Math.random() * 7).toFixed(2) + 's';

            const drift = (Math.random() * 180 - 90).toFixed(1) + 'px';
            const rot = (Math.random() * 720 - 360).toFixed(0) + 'deg';

            const scale = (0.65 + Math.random() * 1.15).toFixed(2);
            const blur = (Math.random() * 1.8).toFixed(1) + 'px';
            const glow = (8 + Math.random() * 26).toFixed(0) + 'px';

            f.style.left = left + 'vw';
            f.style.setProperty('--delay', delay);
            f.style.setProperty('--dur', dur);
            f.style.setProperty('--sway', sway);
            f.style.setProperty('--drift', drift);
            f.style.setProperty('--rot', rot);
            f.style.setProperty('--scale', scale);
            f.style.setProperty('--blur', blur);
            f.style.setProperty('--glow', glow);

            // biar tidak terlalu rata, sebagian masuk dari atas lebih random
            f.style.top = (Math.random() * -25) + 'vh';

            wrap.appendChild(f);
        }
    }
    )();
</script>
</div></div></div></body></html>
